2018-10-30 10:09:54,744 [13] DEBUG IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService [(null)] - IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService.Select@TaskRequest
SELECT TOP 1000 T.[OBJID]
            ,CASE T.[ERR_CODE] WHEN 0 THEN '正常' ELSE '异常' END ERR_CODE
            ,T.[ERR_DESC]
            ,CASE T.[PROC_STATUS] WHEN 0 THEN '等待' WHEN 1 THEN '执行' WHEN 2 THEN '完成' END PROC_STATUS
            ,T.[PROC_CREATE_TIME]
            ,T.[PROC_EXCUTE_TIME]
            ,T.[PROC_FINISH_TIME]
            ,T.[ORDER_TYPE_NO]
            ,T1.LOC_NO SLOC_NO
            ,T2.LOC_NO ELOC_NO
            ,T.[SOURCE_TYPE]
            ,T.[PALLET_NO]
            ,T.[SLOC_TYPE]
            ,T.[SLOC_AREA]
            ,T.[ELOC_TYPE]
            ,CASE T.[PALLET_TYPE] WHEN '1000 'THEN '载货' WHEN '2000' THEN '空载' ELSE '异常' END PALLET_TYPE
            ,T.[ORDER_TYPE_MODULE]
            ,T.[ROUTE_NOS]
            ,T.[PACKAGE_GUID]
            ,T.[TASK_GUID]
            ,T.[TASK_NO]
            ,T.[ELOC_AREA]
        FROM [dbo].[TPROC_0100_TASK_REQUEST] T
        LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC T1 ON T1.LOC_NO = T.SLOC_NO
        LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC T2 ON T2.LOC_NO = T.ELOC_NO
       
      ORDER BY T.OBJID DESC
参数：

@param1=1

2018-10-30 10:09:59,821 [14] DEBUG IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService [(null)] - IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService.Select@CmdRequest
SELECT TOP 1000 T.[OBJID]
            ,CASE T.[ERR_CODE] WHEN 0 THEN '正常' ELSE '异常' END ERR_CODE
            ,T.[ERR_DESC]
            ,CASE T.[PROC_STATUS] WHEN 0 THEN '等待' WHEN 1 THEN '执行' WHEN 2 THEN '完成' END PROC_STATUS
            ,T.[PROC_CREATE_TIME]
            ,T.[PROC_EXCUTE_TIME]
            ,T.[PROC_FINISH_TIME]
            ,T.[TASK_NO]
            ,T.[CURR_LOC_NO]
            ,T.[PALLET_NO]
            ,T.[TASK_GUID]
            ,T.[ROUTE_NO]
            ,T.[ELOC_NO]
            ,T.[PACKAGE_GUID]
            ,T.[IO_TYPE]
            ,T.[TRANSFER_NO]
            ,T.[SLOC_TYPE]
            ,T.[SLOC_AREA]
            ,T.[ELOC_TYPE]
            ,T.[ELOC_AREA]
            ,T.[CMD_OBJID]
        FROM [dbo].[TPROC_0200_CMD_REQUEST] T
        LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC T1 ON T1.LOC_NO = T.CURR_LOC_NO
        LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC T2 ON T2.LOC_NO = T.ELOC_NO
       
      ORDER BY T.OBJID DESC
参数：

SELECT TOP 1000 T.[OBJID]
            ,CASE T.[ERR_CODE] WHEN 0 THEN '正常' ELSE '异常' END ERR_CODE
            ,T.[ERR_DESC]
            ,CASE T.[PROC_STATUS] WHEN 0 THEN '等待' WHEN 1 THEN '执行' WHEN 2 THEN '完成' END PROC_STATUS
            ,T.[PROC_CREATE_TIME]
            ,T.[PROC_EXCUTE_TIME]
            ,T.[PROC_FINISH_TIME]
            ,T.[TASK_NO]
            ,T.[CURR_LOC_NO]
            ,T.[PALLET_NO]
            ,T.[TASK_GUID]
            ,T.[ROUTE_NO]
            ,T.[ELOC_NO]
            ,T.[PACKAGE_GUID]
            ,T.[IO_TYPE]
            ,T.[TRANSFER_NO]
            ,T.[SLOC_TYPE]
            ,T.[SLOC_AREA]
            ,T.[ELOC_TYPE]
            ,T.[ELOC_AREA]
            ,T.[CMD_OBJID]
        FROM [dbo].[TPROC_0200_CMD_REQUEST] T
        LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC T1 ON T1.LOC_NO = T.CURR_LOC_NO
        LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC T2 ON T2.LOC_NO = T.ELOC_NO
       WHERE   T.OBJID =  @param0  
      ORDER BY T.OBJID DESC

@param0=21

2018-10-30 10:15:16,788 [19] DEBUG IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService [(null)] - IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService.Select@TaskRequest
SELECT TOP 1000 T.[OBJID]
            ,CASE T.[ERR_CODE] WHEN 0 THEN '正常' ELSE '异常' END ERR_CODE
            ,T.[ERR_DESC]
            ,CASE T.[PROC_STATUS] WHEN 0 THEN '等待' WHEN 1 THEN '执行' WHEN 2 THEN '完成' END PROC_STATUS
            ,T.[PROC_CREATE_TIME]
            ,T.[PROC_EXCUTE_TIME]
            ,T.[PROC_FINISH_TIME]
            ,T.[ORDER_TYPE_NO]
            ,T1.LOC_NO SLOC_NO
            ,T2.LOC_NO ELOC_NO
            ,T.[SOURCE_TYPE]
            ,T.[PALLET_NO]
            ,T.[SLOC_TYPE]
            ,T.[SLOC_AREA]
            ,T.[ELOC_TYPE]
            ,CASE T.[PALLET_TYPE] WHEN '1000 'THEN '载货' WHEN '2000' THEN '空载' ELSE '异常' END PALLET_TYPE
            ,T.[ORDER_TYPE_MODULE]
            ,T.[ROUTE_NOS]
            ,T.[PACKAGE_GUID]
            ,T.[TASK_GUID]
            ,T.[TASK_NO]
            ,T.[ELOC_AREA]
        FROM [dbo].[TPROC_0100_TASK_REQUEST] T
        LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC T1 ON T1.LOC_NO = T.SLOC_NO
        LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC T2 ON T2.LOC_NO = T.ELOC_NO
       
      ORDER BY T.OBJID DESC
参数：

            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, 
          TL.LIMIT_BIN_NO,
           TL.ELOC_NO,
           TL.LIMIT_PALLET_ID,
           TL.LIMIT_PRODUCT_GUID,
           TL.LIMIT_DATE_START,
           TL.LIMIT_DATE_END,
           TL.DELETE_FLAG,
           TL.ORDER_LINE_GUID,
           TL.LINE_ID,
           TL.SORT_ID,
           TL.MATERIAL_NO,
           TL.REQUIRE_QTY,
           TL.DELETE_FLAG,
           TL.ACT_QTY,
           TL.SHIP_QTY,
           TL.LINE_PRIORITY,
           TL.BIN_ERR_DESC,
           TL.LOCK_END_LOC,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
         WHERE  t1.ORDER_NO =  @param0    
        ORDER BY TL.LINE_ID

2018-10-30 10:26:14,284 [30] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

2018-10-30 10:26:27,435 [25] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BillTaskCmdService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BillTaskCmdService.GetBillDataTable
select TA.*
        from (SELECT CASE t1.ELOC_NO
           WHEN '00000000' THEN
            '立库'
           ELSE
            t3.loc_name
         END AS ELOC_NAME,
         T1.MATERIAL_NO,t1.product_grade,
          T4.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE AS ORDER_TYPE_MODULE1,
         CASE T4.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE
           WHEN 'I' THEN
            '入库'
           WHEN 'O' THEN
            '出库'
           WHEN 'M' THEN
            '移库'
           WHEN 'T' THEN
            '移载'
         END AS ORDER_TYPE_MODULE,
         T1.ORDER_NO,
         T1.LIMIT_BIN_NO,
         T1.ELOC_NO,
         T1.LIMIT_PALLET_ID,
         T1.LIMIT_PRODUCT_GUID,
         T1.CREATION_DATE,
         T1.DELETE_FLAG,
         T1.ORDER_LINE_GUID,
         T1.LINE_ID,
         T1.SORT_ID,
         T1.REQUIRE_QTY,
         T1.ACT_QTY,
         T1.SHIP_QTY,
         T1.BIN_ERR_DESC,
         CASE T1.LOCK_END_LOC
           WHEN 0 THEN
            '未锁定'
           ELSE
            '锁定'
         END AS LOCK_END_LOC,
         T1.Line_Status as LINE_NO,
         CASE T1.LINE_STATUS
           WHEN 0 THEN
            '等待'
           WHEN 1 THEN
            '下达'
           WHEN 2 THEN
            '执行'
           WHEN 3 THEN
            '完成'
           ELSE
            '取消'
         END AS LINE_STATUS,
         T1.LINE_STATUS STATUS
          FROM WBS_ORDER_LINE T1
          LEFT JOIN Psb_Material T2
            ON T1.MATERIAL_NO = T2.MATER_NO
          LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC T3
            ON T1.ELOC_NO = T3.LOC_NO
          LEFT JOIN WBS_ORDER T4
            ON T4.ORDER_NO = T1.ORDER_NO WHERE T1.DELETE_FLAG='N') TA
       WHERE    TA.STATUS >= 0    
        ORDER BY TA.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

2018-10-30 10:26:28,237 [29] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BillTaskCmdService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BillTaskCmdService.GetCmdDataTable
select ta.* from 
          (SELECT T.OBJID,T.TASK_GUID,T.TASK_NO,T.SLOC_PLC_NO,T.ELOC_PLC_NO,
           CASE WHEN T.CMD_TYPE = 'I' THEN '入库' WHEN T.CMD_TYPE = 'O' THEN '出库'
           WHEN T.CMD_TYPE = 'M' THEN '移库'
           ELSE '移载' END CMD_TYPE,
           T.PALLET_NO,T.ROUTE_NO,T.TRANSFER_NO,
           CASE WHEN T.TRANSFER_TYPE = '10' THEN '堆垛机' WHEN T.TRANSFER_TYPE = '20' THEN '输送线' 
           WHEN T.TRANSFER_NO = '30' THEN 'AGV' END TRANSFER_TYPE,
           CASE WHEN T.CMD_STEP = '00' THEN '等待' ELSE '下传' END CMD_STEP,
           T.CREATION_DATE,T.EXCUTE_DATE,T.FINISH_DATE, T1.ORDER_LINE_GUID
      FROM WBS_TASK_CMD T
      LEFT JOIN WBS_TASK T1 ON T1.TASK_GUID = T.TASK_GUID
      UNION ALL
      SELECT T.OBJID,T.TASK_GUID,T.TASK_NO,T.SLOC_PLC_NO,T.ELOC_PLC_NO,
           CASE WHEN T.CMD_TYPE = 'I' THEN '入库' WHEN T.CMD_TYPE = 'O' THEN '出库'
           WHEN T.CMD_TYPE = 'M' THEN '移库' 
           ELSE '移载' END CMD_TYPE,
           T.PALLET_NO,T.ROUTE_NO,T.TRANSFER_NO,
           CASE WHEN T.TRANSFER_TYPE = '10' THEN '堆垛机' WHEN T.TRANSFER_TYPE = '20' THEN '输送线' 
           WHEN T.TRANSFER_NO = '30' THEN 'AGV' END TRANSFER_TYPE,
           '完成' CMD_STEP,
           T.CREATION_DATE,T.EXCUTE_DATE,T.FINISH_DATE, T1.ORDER_LINE_GUID
      FROM Z50_WBS_TASK_CMD T
      LEFT JOIN Z50_WBS_TASK T1 ON T1.TASK_GUID = T.TASK_GUID) ta
       WHERE  TA.ORDER_LINE_GUID = @param0   
      ORDER BY TA.CREATION_DATE
参数：
@param0=Can not Find

2018-10-30 10:26:28,754 [16] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BillTaskCmdService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BillTaskCmdService.GetTaskDataTable
select TA.*
        from (SELECT T.TASK_GUID,T.TASK_NO,T.EMERGENCY,T.SLOC_NO,T.TRANSFER_NO,
                CASE WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'I' THEN '入库' WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'O' THEN '出库' 
                ELSE '移库' END IO_TYPE,
                T.ELOC_NO,T.PALLET_NO,T.PACKAGE_GUID,T.ORDER_LINE_GUID,
                T.SORT_ID,T.CREATION_DATE, T.TASK_EXEC_START_DT,T.TASK_EXEC_END_DT,
                CASE WHEN T.TASK_STEP = '0000' THEN '等待' ELSE '执行' END TASK_STEP, 
                T.ROUTE_NOS,T.UNEXE_ROUTE_NO,T.FINISH_DESC,T1.MATER_NO,1 USE_QTY
          FROM WBS_TASK T
          LEFT JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1
            ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
        UNION ALL
        SELECT T.TASK_GUID,T.TASK_NO,T.EMERGENCY,T.SLOC_NO,T.TRANSFER_NO,
                CASE WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'I' THEN '入库' WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'O' THEN '出库' 
                ELSE '移库' END IO_TYPE,
                T.ELOC_NO,T.PALLET_NO,T.PACKAGE_GUID,T.ORDER_LINE_GUID,
                T.SORT_ID,T.CREATION_DATE, T.TASK_EXEC_START_DT,T.TASK_EXEC_END_DT,
                '完成' TASK_STEP, T.ROUTE_NOS,T.UNEXE_ROUTE_NO,T.FINISH_DESC,
                ISNULL(T1.MATER_NO,T2.MATER_NO) MATERIAL_NO,
                1 USE_QTY
          FROM Z50_WBS_TASK T
          LEFT JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1
            ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
          LEFT JOIN Z50_WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T2
            ON T2.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID ) TA
       WHERE  TA.ORDER_LINE_GUID = @param0   
      ORDER BY TA.CREATION_DATE
参数：
@param0=Can not Find

2018-10-30 10:26:39,976 [29] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.TaskService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.TaskService.GetTaskData
SELECT T.TASK_GUID,T.TASK_NO,
                CASE T.IO_TYPE WHEN 'I' THEN '入库' WHEN 'O' THEN '出库' WHEN 'M' THEN '移库' ELSE '移载' END IO_TYPE,
                T.TRANSFER_NO,
                ISNULL(T2.BIN_PLC_NO,T3.LOC_PLC_NO) SLOC_NO,
                ISNULL(T4.BIN_PLC_NO,T5.LOC_PLC_NO) ELOC_NO,
                T.PALLET_NO,T.CREATION_DATE,T.TASK_EXEC_END_DT,
                ISNULL(T1.OBJID,0) OBJID,T1.SLOC_PLC_NO,T1.ELOC_PLC_NO,
                T1.TRANSFER_NO EQUIP_NO,
                CASE WHEN T1.CMD_STEP = '00' THEN '等待' WHEN T1.CMD_STEP = '02' THEN '执行' WHEN T1.CMD_STEP IS NULL THEN '未生成指令' END CMD_STEP
          FROM WBS_TASK T
          LEFT JOIN WBS_TASK_CMD T1
            ON T1.TASK_GUID = T.TASK_GUID
          LEFT JOIN PSB_BIN_STATUS T2
            ON T2.BIN_NO = T.SLOC_NO
          LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC T3
            ON T3.LOC_NO = T.SLOC_NO
          LEFT JOIN PSB_BIN_STATUS T4
            ON T4.BIN_NO = T.ELOC_NO
          LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC T5
            ON T5.LOC_NO = T.ELOC_NO
          WHERE 1=1
           
      ORDER BY T1.CREATION_DATE 
参数：

2018-10-30 10:30:05,663 [32] DEBUG IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService [(null)] - IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService.Select@Z50WbsTaskCmd
SELECT TOP 1000 T.OBJID,
            T.TASK_NO,
            CASE T.CMD_TYPE WHEN 'I' THEN '入库' WHEN 'O' THEN '出库' ELSE '移载' END AS CMD_TYPE,
            T.SLOC_NO,
            T.ELOC_NO,
            T.SLOC_PLC_NO,
            T.ELOC_PLC_NO,
            T.CREATION_DATE,
            T.EXCUTE_DATE,
            T.FINISH_DATE,
            T1.MATER_NO,
            T1.MATER_NAME,
            T.ROUTE_NO,
            T.TRANSFER_NO,
            T.FINISH_STATUS,
            T.PALLET_NO,
            T.ORDER_LINE_GUID,
            CASE T.CMD_STEP WHEN '00' THEN '指令生成' WHEN '02' THEN '指令下传' ELSE '异常' END AS CMD_STEP,
            T.PACKAGE_GUID,
            T.ERR_NO,
            T.ERR_NAME
            FROM Z50_WBS_TASK_CMD T
            LEFT JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1
              ON T.PACKAGE_GUID = T1.PACKAGE_GUID
        WHERE 1=1
        AND  T.CREATION_DATE <= 1+ @param0    
      ORDER BY T.OBJID DESC
参数：
@param0=2018/10/30 0:00:00

2018-10-30 10:33:34,710 [25] DEBUG IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService [(null)] - IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService.Select@Z50WbsTaskCmd@MainDetail
SELECT T.OBJID,
            T.TASK_NO,
            CASE T.CMD_TYPE WHEN 'I' THEN '入库' WHEN 'O' THEN '出库' ELSE '移载' END AS CMD_TYPE,
            T.SLOC_NO,
            T.ELOC_NO,
            T.SLOC_PLC_NO,
            T.ELOC_PLC_NO,
            T.CREATION_DATE,
            T.EXCUTE_DATE,
            T.FINISH_DATE,
            T1.MATER_NO,
            T1.MATER_NAME,
            T.ROUTE_NO,
            T.TRANSFER_NO,
            T.FINISH_STATUS,
            T.PALLET_NO,
            T.ORDER_LINE_GUID,
            CASE T.CMD_STEP WHEN '00' THEN '指令生成' WHEN '02' THEN '指令下传' ELSE '异常' END AS CMD_STEP,
            T.PACKAGE_GUID,
            T.ERR_NO,
            T.ERR_NAME
            FROM Z50_WBS_TASK_CMD T
            LEFT JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1
              ON T.PACKAGE_GUID = T1.PACKAGE_GUID
        WHERE 1=1
参数：

2018-10-30 10:35:50,684 [25] DEBUG IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService [(null)] - IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService.Select@SearchPalletData
SELECT T.PALLET_NO, T.PALLET_NO PALLET_NAME,
        CASE WHEN T1.MATER_NO IS NOT NULL THEN T1.MATER_NO
        WHEN T1.MATER_NO IS NULL AND T.LOAD_STATUS = 0 THEN '空工装'
        ELSE '绑定异常' END MATER_NO
        FROM PSB_PALLET T 
        LEFT JOIN PSB_PRODUCT T1 ON T1.PRODUCT_GUID = T.PRODUCT_GUID
        WHERE T.DELETE_FLAG = 0
       
      ORDER BY T.PALLET_NO
参数：

2018-10-30 10:36:10,972 [22] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.TaskService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.TaskService.GetTaskData
SELECT T.TASK_GUID,T.TASK_NO,
                CASE T.IO_TYPE WHEN 'I' THEN '入库' WHEN 'O' THEN '出库' WHEN 'M' THEN '移库' ELSE '移载' END IO_TYPE,
                T.TRANSFER_NO,
                ISNULL(T2.BIN_PLC_NO,T3.LOC_PLC_NO) SLOC_NO,
                ISNULL(T4.BIN_PLC_NO,T5.LOC_PLC_NO) ELOC_NO,
                T.PALLET_NO,T.CREATION_DATE,T.TASK_EXEC_END_DT,
                ISNULL(T1.OBJID,0) OBJID,T1.SLOC_PLC_NO,T1.ELOC_PLC_NO,
                T1.TRANSFER_NO EQUIP_NO,
                CASE WHEN T1.CMD_STEP = '00' THEN '等待' WHEN T1.CMD_STEP = '02' THEN '执行' WHEN T1.CMD_STEP IS NULL THEN '未生成指令' END CMD_STEP
          FROM WBS_TASK T
          LEFT JOIN WBS_TASK_CMD T1
            ON T1.TASK_GUID = T.TASK_GUID
          LEFT JOIN PSB_BIN_STATUS T2
            ON T2.BIN_NO = T.SLOC_NO
          LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC T3
            ON T3.LOC_NO = T.SLOC_NO
          LEFT JOIN PSB_BIN_STATUS T4
            ON T4.BIN_NO = T.ELOC_NO
          LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC T5
            ON T5.LOC_NO = T.ELOC_NO
          WHERE 1=1
           
      ORDER BY T1.CREATION_DATE 
参数：

2018-10-30 10:36:48,644 [22] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.TaskService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.TaskService.GetCrnForkErrorStatus
 
        SELECT FS.CRN_NO,
              FS.CRN_FORK_NO,
              FS.TASK_NO,
              CASE FS.TASK_TYPE WHEN 'I' THEN '入库' WHEN 'M' THEN '移库' ELSE '出库' END AS TASK_TYPE,
                CASE WHEN T2.ERR_NAME IS NULL THEN '正常' ELSE T2.ERR_NAME END AS FAULT_NAME,
              FS.FROM_BIN,FS.TO_BIN,FS.ACT_POS_X,FS.ACT_POS_Y,
              FS.FIP_FAULT_NO,
              FS.FIP_DATE,
              FS.FIP_HANDLE_RESULT,
              CASE FS.FIP_FLAG WHEN 0 THEN '正常' WHEN 1 THEN '待确认' WHEN 2 THEN '已确认' WHEN 3 THEN '已处理' END AS FIP_FLAG
        FROM PEM_CRN_FORK_STATUS FS 
        LEFT JOIN PSB_CRN_ERR T2 ON FS.FAULT_NO = T2.ERR_NO
       ORDER BY FS.CRN_NO,FS.CRN_FORK_NO

      INNER JOIN V_SSP_USER_ALL_ACTION t2 ON t2.ACTION_ID = t1.OBJID

2018-10-30 10:38:57,456 [22] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BinDataService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BinDataService.GetErrBinNo
SELECT T.*,
              CASE WHEN T.BIN_BIZ_STATUS = 'E' THEN '空出库'
                   WHEN T.BIN_BIZ_STATUS = 'P' THEN '先入品'
                   WHEN T.BIN_STATUS != '_' AND T1.PACKAGE_GUID IS NULL THEN '库位有货,库存无记录'
                   WHEN T.BIN_STATUS = '_' AND T1.PACKAGE_GUID IS NOT NULL THEN '库位无货,库存有信息'
                   WHEN T.BIN_BIZ_STATUS = 'I' THEN '入库占用异常'
                   WHEN T.BIN_BIZ_STATUS = 'O' THEN '出库占用异常'
               END ERR_NAME
              FROM PSB_BIN_STATUS T
              LEFT JOIN WBS_BIN T1
                ON T1.BIN_NO = T.BIN_NO
             WHERE T.BIN_BIZ_STATUS IN ('E','P')
                OR (T.BIN_STATUS != '_' AND T1.PACKAGE_GUID IS NULL)
                OR (T.BIN_STATUS = '_' AND T1.PACKAGE_GUID IS NOT NULL)
                OR (T.BIN_BIZ_STATUS IN ('I','O') AND NOT EXISTS

2018-10-30 10:39:06,590 [26] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BinDataService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BinDataService.GetProductStatistics
 
        SELECT TA.*,CONVERT(VARCHAR,ROUND(TA.FG_BIN/TA.TOTAL_BIN,2)*100)+'%' AS USE_RATE,
        CONVERT(VARCHAR,(1-ROUND(TA.DISA_BIN/TA.TOTAL_BIN,2))*100)+'%' AS STO_RATE FROM (
        SELECT * FROM (SELECT TOP 99.9999 PERCENT CONVERT(VARCHAR, T.Real_Group_No) AS ROW_NO,
        COUNT(CASE T.BIN_STATUS WHEN CHAR(36) THEN 1 ELSE NULL END) AS FG_BIN,	-------------物料
        COUNT(CASE T.BIN_STATUS WHEN  '_' THEN 1 ELSE NULL END) AS EMPTY_BIN,   -------------空库位
        COUNT(CASE T.USED_FLAG WHEN 0 THEN 1 ELSE NULL END) AS DISA_BIN,		-------------禁用库位
        (COUNT(CASE T.BIN_BIZ_STATUS WHEN 'P' THEN 1 ELSE NULL END)
        + COUNT(CASE T.BIN_BIZ_STATUS WHEN 'E' THEN 1 ELSE NULL END))
        AS ERR_BIN,																-------------异常库位(空出库位，先入库位)
        (COUNT(CASE T.BIN_BIZ_STATUS WHEN 'I' THEN 1 ELSE NULL END)
        + COUNT(CASE T.BIN_BIZ_STATUS WHEN 'O' THEN 1 ELSE NULL END))
        AS RES_BIN,																-------------预约库位
        COUNT(*) AS TOTAL_BIN,
		T.Real_Group_No
        FROM PSB_BIN_STATUS T
        GROUP BY  T.Real_Group_No
		ORDER BY T.Real_Group_No) T1								-------------总库位
        UNION  
        SELECT * FROM (SELECT TOP 99.9999 PERCENT '总计' AS ROW_NO,
        COUNT(CASE BIN_STATUS WHEN CHAR(36) THEN 1 ELSE NULL END) AS FG_BIN,				-------------物料
        COUNT(CASE BIN_STATUS WHEN '_' THEN 1 ELSE NULL END) AS EMPTY_BIN,					-------------空库位
        COUNT(CASE T.USED_FLAG WHEN 0 THEN 1 ELSE NULL END) AS DISA_BIN,					-------------禁用库位
        (  COUNT(CASE BIN_BIZ_STATUS WHEN 'P' THEN 1 ELSE NULL END)
        + COUNT(CASE BIN_BIZ_STATUS WHEN 'E' THEN 1 ELSE NULL END))
        AS ERR_BIN,																-------------异常库位(空出库位，先入库位)
        (COUNT(CASE T.BIN_BIZ_STATUS WHEN 'I' THEN 1 ELSE NULL END)
        + COUNT(CASE T.BIN_BIZ_STATUS WHEN 'O' THEN 1 ELSE NULL END))
        AS RES_BIN,																-------------预约库位
        COUNT(*) AS TOTAL_BIN,
		99999999 AS Real_Group_No
        FROM PSB_BIN_STATUS T 
		) T2
		) TA
		ORDER BY  Real_Group_No

2018-10-30 10:39:21,696 [19] DEBUG IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService [(null)] - IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService.Select@BinData
SELECT T.BIN_NO
              ,T.CREATION_DATE
              ,CASE T2.BIN_STATUS WHEN CHAR(36) THEN '正常' ELSE '异常' END BIN_STATUS
              ,CASE T2.BIN_BIZ_STATUS WHEN '_' THEN '在库' WHEN 'O' THEN '预约出库' WHEN 'I' THEN '预约入库' WHEN 'M' THEN '移库' ELSE '其他' END BIN_BIZ_STATUS
              ,T.PALLET_NO
              ,T1.MATER_NO
              ,T1.MATER_NAME
              ,T1.PRODUCT_GUID
              ,T1.PRODUCT_DATE
              ,T1.PRODUCT_QTY
              ,T1.MAIN_UNIT
         FROM WBS_BIN T
         LEFT JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1 ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
         LEFT JOIN PSB_BIN_STATUS T2 ON T2.BIN_NO = T.BIN_NO
       where   T.CREATION_DATE >= @param0    AND  T.CREATION_DATE <= 1+ @param1
参数：
@param0=2017/10/29 0:00:00
@param1=2018/10/30 0:00:00

2018-10-30 10:40:15,991 [19] DEBUG IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService [(null)] - IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService.Select@BinData@MainDetail
SELECT T.BIN_NO
              ,T.CREATION_DATE
              ,CASE T2.BIN_STATUS WHEN CHAR(36) THEN '正常' ELSE '异常' END BIN_STATUS
              ,CASE T2.BIN_BIZ_STATUS WHEN 'O' THEN '预约出库' WHEN 'I' THEN '预约入库' WHEN 'M' THEN '移库' ELSE '其他' END BIN_BIZ_STATUS
              ,T.PALLET_NO
              ,T1.MATER_NO
              ,T1.MATER_NAME
              ,T1.PRODUCT_GUID
              ,T1.PRODUCT_DATE
              ,T1.PRODUCT_QTY
              ,T1.MAIN_UNIT
         FROM WBS_BIN T
         LEFT JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1 ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
         LEFT JOIN PSB_BIN_STATUS T2 ON T2.BIN_NO = T.BIN_NO
       WHERE   T.BIN_NO =  @param0

@param0=03450901

2018-10-30 10:41:07,834 [19] DEBUG IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService [(null)] - IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService.Select@InOutBinHistory
SELECT T.BIN_GUID,
        T.BIN_NO,
        CASE WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'I' THEN '入库'
             WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'O' THEN '出库'
        END IO_TYPE,
        T.CREATION_DATE,
        T.PALLET_NO,
        ISNULL(T1.MATER_NO,T2.MATER_NO) MATER_NO,
        ISNULL(T1.MATER_NAME,T2.MATER_NAME) MATER_NAME,
        CASE WHEN T.FINISH_FLAG IS NULL OR T.FINISH_FLAG = '_' THEN '正常'
        ELSE T.FINISH_FLAG END FINISH_FLAG,
        CASE WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'I' THEN ISNULL(T3.SLOC_NO,T4.SLOC_NO)
             WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'O' THEN ISNULL(T3.ELOC_NO,T4.ELOC_NO) 
        END LOC_NO,
        ISNULL(T3.TASK_NO,T4.TASK_NO) TASK_NO,
        ISNULL(T3.CREATION_DATE,T4.CREATION_DATE) CREATE_TASK_DATE,
        ISNULL(T3.TASK_EXEC_START_DT,T4.TASK_EXEC_START_DT) TASK_EXEC_START_DT,
        ISNULL(T3.TASK_EXEC_END_DT,T4.TASK_EXEC_END_DT) TASK_EXEC_END_DT
        FROM Z50_WBS_BIN T
        LEFT JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1 ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
        LEFT JOIN Z50_WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T2 ON T2.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
        LEFT JOIN WBS_TASK T3 ON T3.TASK_GUID = T.TASK_GUID
        LEFT JOIN Z50_WBS_TASK T4 ON T4.TASK_GUID = T.TASK_GUID
       where   T.CREATION_DATE >= @param0    AND  T.CREATION_DATE <= 1+ @param1
参数：
@param0=2018/10/25 0:00:00
@param1=2018/10/30 0:00:00

SELECT T.BIN_NO,T.PALLET_NO,T1.MATER_NO MATERIAL_NO,T1.MATER_SPEC,ISNULL(T1.PRODUCT_QTY,1) as QTY,T1.PRODUCT_DATE
